tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n \xc4\x91\xe1\xba\xa1i h\xe1\xbb\x8dc theo ph\xc6\xb0\xc6\xa1ng th\xe1\xbb\xa9c tr\xe1\xbb\xb1c tuy\xe1\xba\xbfn.</p>\n\n<p><strong>T\xe1\xbb\xab ng\xc3\xa0y 19/9 \xc4\x91\xe1\xba\xbfn 17 gi\xe1\xbb\x9d ng\xc3\xa0y 27/9:\xc2\xa0</strong>Th\xc3\xad sinh \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u\xc2\xa0ch\xe1\xbb\x89nh nguy\xe1\xbb\x87n v\xe1\xbb\x8dng \xc4\x91\xc4\x83ng k\xc3\xbd x\xc3\xa9t tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n \xc4\x91\xe1\xba\xa1i h\xe1\xbb\x8dc b\xe1\xba\xb1ng Phi\xe1\xba\xbfu \xc4\x91\xc4\x83ng k\xc3\xbd x\xc3\xa9t tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n.</p>\n\n<p><strong>Tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9bc 17 gi\xe1\xbb\x9d ng\xc3\xa0y 29/9:\xc2\xa0</strong>Th\xc3\xad sinh ki\xe1\xbb\x83m tra k\xe1\xba\xbft qu\xe1\xba\xa3 \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u ch\xe1\xbb\x89nh nguy\xe1\xbb\x87n v\xe1\xbb\x8dng \xc4\x91\xc4\x83ng k\xc3\xbd x\xc3\xa9t tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n v\xc3\xa0 \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\x81 ngh\xe1\xbb\x8b \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u ch\xe1\xbb\x89nh sai s\xc3\xb3t n\xe1\xba\xbfu c\xc3\xb3 (ch\xe1\xbb\x89 \xc3\xa1p d\xe1\xbb\xa5ng \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\x91i v\xe1\xbb\x9bi th\xc3\xad sinh \xc4\x91i\xe1\xbb\x81u ch\xe1\xbb\x89nh nguy\xe1\xbb\x87n v\xe1\xbb\x8dng \xc4\x91\xc4\x83ng k\xc3\xbd x\xc3\xa9t tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n b\xe1\xba\xb1ng phi\xe1\xba\xbfu).</p>\n\n<p><strong>Tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9bc 17 gi\xe1\xbb\x9d ng\xc3\xa0y 05/10:\xc2\xa0</strong>C\xc3\xa1c tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9dng c\xc3\xb4ng b\xe1\xbb\x91 k\xe1\xba\xbft qu\xe1\xba\xa3 tr\xc3\xbang tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\xa3t 1.</p>\n\n<p><strong>Tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9bc 17 gi\xe1\xbb\x9d ng\xc3\xa0y 10/10:\xc2\xa0</strong>\xc2\xa0Th\xc3\xad sinh x\xc3\xa1c nh\xe1\xba\xadn nh\xe1\xba\xadp h\xe1\xbb\x8dc \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\xa3t 1.</p>\n\n<p><strong>T\xe1\xbb\xab ng\xc3\xa0y 15/10:\xc2\xa0</strong>C\xc3\xa1c tr\xc6\xb0\xe1\xbb\x9dng c\xc3\xb2n thi\xe1\xba\xbfu ch\xe1\xbb\x89 ti\xc3\xaau b\xe1\xba\xaft \xc4\x91\xe1\xba\xa7u nh\xe1\xba\xadn h\xe1\xbb\x93 s\xc6\xa1 x\xc3\xa9t tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n \xc4\x91\xe1\xbb\xa3t b\xe1\xbb\x95 sung.</p>\n</div>\n<div class="panel panel-primary">\n\t<div class="panel-heading">\n\t\tTin Tuy\xe1\xbb\x83n sinh
